<div id="review_1538571989" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1538571989" />
    <a title="Ally" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15655618-ally"><img alt="Ally" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1472122701p2/15655618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1538571989?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ally" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ally" href="/user/show/15655618-ally">Ally</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781409159353" href="/book/show/27255774-glass-sword">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1538571989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8457442219351464511">£10.99 for a <i>paperback</i>?!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439062779ra/15790832.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Completely and totally not worth the money. Luckily I borrowed a copy. I could not bring myself to spend money on this and boy am I glad I went with my instincts on this one. What a fucking <i>terrible</i> book. <br/><br/><b>If I am a sword, I am a sword made of glass, and I feel myself beginning to shatter.</b><br/><br/>I'm really not exaggerating when I say I hated this. I strongly disliked <i>Red Queen</i> but there were enjoyable moments. But while reading <i>Glass Sword</i> I could literally feel my life ebbing aw</span>
  <span id="freeText8457442219351464511" style="display:none">£10.99 for a <i>paperback</i>?!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439062779ra/15790832.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Completely and totally not worth the money. Luckily I borrowed a copy. I could not bring myself to spend money on this and boy am I glad I went with my instincts on this one. What a fucking <i>terrible</i> book. <br><br><b>If I am a sword, I am a sword made of glass, and I feel myself beginning to shatter.</b><br><br>I'm really not exaggerating when I say I hated this. I strongly disliked <i>Red Queen</i> but there were enjoyable moments. But while reading <i>Glass Sword</i> I could literally feel my life ebbing away. My organs were shutting down, I was losing brain function. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433596894ra/15117562.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I do not understand the hype for this book. I just can't wrap my head around it. It's <i>all over</i> my Tumblr feed. It's <i>everywhere</i> on Twitter. Other readers are losing their shit over Mare Barrow's predicament and yet, here I am struggling to find a single fuck to give. Victoria Aveyard must have one <i>hellavu</i> marketing team behind her. Or maybe I just missed something. I couldn't find a single page in <i>Glass Sword</i> that warrants the anticipation and reception this book has received. I mean, looks like <i>Red Queen</i> is gonna be a freaking movie? You can read more about that <a href="http://screenrant.com/red-queen-books-movie-elizabeth-banks/" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>. I am confused and uncomfortable because I feel like everyone else is seeing something that I'm not. What is it about this series that's getting people so fucking excited? <br><br><i>The average rating for this is 4.27 !!!</i> What's that about? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455640713ra/18130279.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>We pick up where we left off with Mare and the gang having narrowly escaped losing their lives to the Silver court. From there on out it's just <i>running</i>, endless running as they search for the prized newbloods, in a race against Maven to gain the upper hand. <br><br>My biggest beef with <i>Glass Sword</i> is Mare. I fucking hate her. Like, I <i>loath</i> her. She's a jumped up, arrogant, nasty piece of work. <br><br><b>Part of me wants to hold my ground, to stand, to fight. My purple-and-white lightening will certainly make me a target and draw the jets away from the fleeing Guard. I might even take a plane or two with me. But that cannot be. I'm worth more than the rest, more than red masks and bandages.</b><br><br>From this moment on, I knew Mare and I would never see eye to eye. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455643207ra/18130784.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I get that she has a revolution to partake in. I understand that that means making some tough choices and stepping up to the challenge of becoming a leader who can shoulder the burden of these difficult decisions. But what I don't understand is this deep rooted <i>arrogance</i>. She's a power crazy bitch. Let's all just keep in mind that Mare has been aware of her abilities for one month. Yes, <i>one month</i>. Prior to that month she was scraping coins together in some godforsaken crap hole with barely the wherewithal to look before she crossed the fucking street. Now, she's been transformed into some freaking goddess, commanding Zeus himself with her incredible prowess as lightening wielder. All after barely more schooling than a few etiquette lessons and a couple of history classes.<br><br>She reminds me of one of the know-all kids that we all remember from our school days, muscling in on every discussion because she read some Wikipedia article that makes her an insta-expert on everything and anything. <i>Please</i> . . . <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393519373ra/8726015.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, so she's got her little lightening trick. Fine. But she's basically an untrained street-rat. And yet she takes it upon herself to head a fucking revolution. I kept waiting for someone to tell her to pipe the fuck down. I mean, what she's trying to achieve is tantamount to attempting to perform brain surgery after managing to successfully stick a plaster over a friend's grazed knee. But no, Mare apparently has morphed overnight into superwoman extraordinaire:<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455643207ra/18130785.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some interesting things I learned about electricity in <i>Glass Sword</i>: <br>-It can be used to destroy metal<br>-it can be used to create a forcefield <br>-It can be used to break a fall<br>-It can be used to blast things into a million pieces<br>-It can be used in place of duct tape for just about anything you can think of<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435942686ra/15395475.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mare is such a fucking <i>special snowflake</i>. She's elevated to god-like heights in this book and it's just all so fucking <i>convenient</i>. <br><br><b>My ability is my most prized possession, even though it separates me from everyone else. But for power, for my own power, it is a price I am willing to pay.</b><br><br>Mare's ability separates her from everyone else because she places herself in a prison of her own making. She's so fucking up herself she alienates everyone around her. If she tried maybe getting that ego in check, she may find people gravitate more towards her. But instead, she plays the martyr. She puts up this hideous cold, uninviting front and creates a self fulfilling prophesy whereby she assumes no one wants to be close to her because she's so different and she's so special and actually end up pushing everyone away. She pushed <i>me</i> away. I couldn't stand the bitch.<br><br>She's got a lot of guilt on her shoulders, she's responsible for the deaths of many people, she has to make choices that end up hurting a few for the greater good. Fine, she's got a struggle, a cross to bear. But where Katniss was endearing and relatable in her similar ethical and moral dilemma, Mare is like a punch in the face. She's a bulldozer. She plows into every scenario the gang find themselves in, dragging her delusion of grandeur behind her, with a big flashing neon sign over her head stating: <i>I'm special. Look at me. LOOK AT ME.</i> Insufferable. And she's not even amusing or interesting with it. <br><br>I absolutely <i>loved</i> reading about Carswell Thorne in <i>The Lunar Chronicles</i> because he's got this massive ego, insists everyone calls him captain though he's done nothing to earn that title besides stealing a ship and generally thinks he's god's gift to women. But he's lighthearted about it. His head is as big as a planet but he doesn't drown in his own self importance because unlike Mare, he isn't also mopey and self involved. Mare's head is so far up her own ass, I'm surprised she can even see where she's going. Her voice is incredibly grating. We're were never going to be off to a winner as the book is written in first person present tense but it's also so pretentious and over written, peppered with this almost <i>constant</i> inner monologue I wanted to rip out my own eyes and stomp on them. <br><br><b>I’m safer than I’ve been in days, surrounded by the people I love most, and yet I’ve never wanted to cry more. For them, I hold back. I curl inward and bleed alone, inside, where no one else can see.</b><br><br>Shut up.<br><br><b>Mare of the Stilts died the day she fell onto a lightning shield. Mareena, the lost Silver princess, died in the Bowl of Bones. And I don’t know what new person opened her eyes on the Undertrain. I only know what she has been and what she has lost, and the weight of it is almost crushing.</b><br><br>Okay, you need to stop now. <br><br><b>While they stand with me, there's no-one beside me. Even with an army at my back, I'm still alone.</b> <br><br>Dear god, someone make it <i>stop</i>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455651403ra/18132130.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some of the writing is so cringe it hurts me, it <i>physically</i> hurts me. The rest of is just incredibly uncomfortable, over dramatic and feels like something straight out of a very important creative writing class where no-one talks, but sits hunched over their laptop trying desperately to out-write the student sitting next to them. The effect is, the writing creates this barrier between Mare and reader. She's so stiff she's like a day old corpse in the throes of rigor mortis. I could find nothing to relate to. I understand that the tone of the book is very serious. A revolution and a race against time to save lives is nothing to laugh about, but there's gotta be some kind of reprieve where we can breathe and smile at each other. Otherwise readers end up finishing the book and immediately require a chiropractor to work out all those kinks now formed in their shoulder muscles. Give us some kind of break where we can see Mare as a human being that we can actually warm to rather than either a scorpion waiting to strike, or a blubbering mess of jello puddled on the floor. There's nothing genuine or likeable about Mare. She's simply horribly contrived and awkward. I really detested her. <br><br>I can hate characters because they're dumb shits but to also find a book where the writing just sets my teeth on edge? I got <i>real</i> unlucky. That's two strikes. Three strikes and you're out right? Yeah, <i>Glass Sword</i> is out. The third strike's a biggie:<br><br><i>Nothing happens</i><br><br>This book is violently, almost <i>abusively</i> boring. <br><br>90% of it is dedicated to Mare swanning about moping and lamenting her inner turmoil, stating how <i>cruel</i> she is, how <i>different</i> she is, how much of an <i>outsider</i> she's <s>made herself</s> become. Okay, I get that she has trust issues. She's been let down. <i>Big time</i>. But on closer inspection, Mare is surrounded by many loyal friends: Kilorn, Farley, even Cal has made a commitment to help her. And yet she's fixated on being alone and trusting no-one: <br><br><b>Anyone, anything, can betray anyone. Even your own heart.</b><br><br><i>Get over yourself, Mare.</i> Shit happens. You suck it up and you fucking move on. And maybe you actually do something other than glower and stomp about. The remaining 10% of the book is simply emotionally manipulative and badly described running, jumping and searching. <br><br>A lot of the book is incredibly difficult to picture. There's no map. Not a deal breaker, but it would have made life easier considering there are several locations. What <i>is</i> a deal breaker however, is a complete lack of cohesive telling when it came to action sequences. I had no fucking clue what was going on half the time because the scene setting was abysmal. The scenes which should have been real turning points in the story arc went off like damp fire works. It was just bad. The deaths had zero impact. I literally gave not a single fuck. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455652504ra/18132347.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The only thing that I found mildly shocking was Mare's treatment of Queen Elana's body. She killed her. Fine. Maybe even good. Queen Elana was a twisted, sadistic bitch. But Mare then proceeds to stoop to her level by severing Queen Elana's head and holding it up like some vile trophy during her broadcast. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404530ra/787244.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, Mare is supposed to be a grey area character with questionable actions. But that is sub-human. An act like that is beyond wrong and was completely unnecessary. Mare could have been portrayed as cruel and vengeful in far more skilful, subtle and powerful ways than this absurd show of defiling a dead body. Have some pride, for the love of god. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>When you feel such a strong repulsion towards a main character as I feel towards Mare, there's really no hope. Even Cal, who was actually alright in <i>Glass Sword</i> was lost in the shit storm that is Mare Barrow. She eclipsed everything that could have been mildly tolerable. I couldn't see past the red veil of rage I felt more strongly with each page I turned. I just wanted to:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455741713ra/18145133.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do you know what we <i>have</i> to talk about? The fucking <i>dead baby</i>. This is where emotional manipulation rears it's ugly head. There was absolutely <i>zero</i> reason to place that in there. It added nothing to the story, nothing to the character development. <i>Ooh, look how evil the Silvers are, they murdered a baby</i>. Okay, but what about the <i>adults</i> they murdered? Are we just gonna glance at those bodies hanging in the square and fucking sashay away? Are they of lesser value, less worthy of our grief just because they are fully grown men and women? I didn't see anyone vomiting in the fucking fireplace when we stumbled upon <i>those</i> mutilated corpses. It was redundant and it was a cheap shot tug at the heart strings. I do not approve. <br><br>I think a lot of the reason why this book has inspired so much rage in me is not the fact that it's a terrible book. Shit happens and you read some crap and you move on. But when a book is built up to be this incredible work of literature worth losing your fucking mind over, <i>worth spending thousands and thousands of dollars making a movie of</i>, when people are going wild for it and throwing edits around and hyping it to the highest of heights and then it turns out to be an actual pile of garbage? It seems unfair to be honest. It's unfair on all the books that are lesser known, that I have read and are wonderful. Books that I simply stumbled upon because they haven't had half the exposure books like <i>Glass Sword</i> have gotten. There's nothing unique about this series. We've seen in all before. We've read <i>The Hunger Games</i>, we've watched <i>X-Men</i>. So what is it that makes this book more worthy of such anticipation than all the droves of other books that are, well, just <i>better</i>? I find this frustrating and I swear to all the gods, if I so much as <i>glance</i> at the third instalment of this series, someone place a gun to my head and promise to pull that fucking trigger if I don't back away slowly. <i>Do it</i>. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8457442219351464511" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1193075814" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1193075814?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1193075814" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15714052505842857502">| ARC kindly provided by Orion Publishing Group via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review. Thank you a lot! |<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>Blurb:</b> Mare Barrow’s blood is red—the color of common folk—but her Silver ability, the power to control lightning, has turned her into a weapon that the royal court tries to control. <br/>The crown calls her an impossibility, a fake, but as she makes her escape from Maven, the prince—the friend—who betrayed her, Mare uncovers something startling: she is not the only one of her kind.<br/>Pursue</span>
  <span id="freeText15714052505842857502" style="display:none">| ARC kindly provided by Orion Publishing Group via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review. Thank you a lot! |<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Blurb:</b> Mare Barrow’s blood is red—the color of common folk—but her Silver ability, the power to control lightning, has turned her into a weapon that the royal court tries to control. <br>The crown calls her an impossibility, a fake, but as she makes her escape from Maven, the prince—the friend—who betrayed her, Mare uncovers something startling: she is not the only one of her kind.<br>Pursued by Maven, now a vindictive king, Mare sets out to find and recruit other Red-and-Silver fighters to join in the struggle against her oppressors. <br>But Mare finds herself on a deadly path, at risk of becoming exactly the kind of monster she is trying to defeat. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451762662ra/17599951.gif" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After a few days where I was supposed to make peace with certain things that happened in this book, I’ve come with the following conclusion:<br><br><u>I have no idea how the fuck I’m supposed to feel about this story and I’m this close to give up on the whole thing.</u><br><br>I’m utterly disappointed in Aveyard, to be quite honest. She had a chance to redeem herself with this book and she just threw it away. There were only two things I liked about this story and I’ll talk about them later. Let me explain why this turned out a disaster for me.<br><br>Alright, you may not remember but when I finished reading <i>Red Queen</i> I said I needed Mare to level up and start being a cunning girl. She has potential but when it comes to explore she either is afraid or messes it up.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389601479ra/8043362.gif" width="500" height="237" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I could not stand her at all.</b> She was low <s>HIGH</s> key in a never ending sorry fest that had me wanting to stab her for like 99% of the book. I just didn’t get her! WHY WAS SHE MOPPING ABOUT? <i>Oh, poor Mare, she was fooled by Maven. Oh, poor little girl, she was hurt. Sweet innocent child can’t trust anyone…</i> I had to put the book down more than 7 times just because of her and her effing whining attitude.<br><br>Oh, when she tried to be “bad-ass”? Whining tough wannabe. Mare was such a great disappointment my brain cannot wrap about how stupid she was during the whole book. I’m speechless.<br><br>Now, I’d like to say something nice about her but I did not find anything and I have no motivation to just go ahead and try to search for something decent to say. Nope, just no. It was plain stupid how she was pinning after Maven. She had to fucking move on but keeping those letters? Stupid ass decision. <br><br><b>
  <u>EVERYTHING ABOUT MARE WAS DUMB AND DISSAPOINTING.</u>
</b> She was just a little girl trying to play the ruthless boss.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451762662ra/17599950.gif" width="500" height="255" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If there was something I hated the same or even more than Mare dumb as fuck Barrow was those tag lines and nicknames. <br><br>Oh my god, I could find the words <i>Lightning girl, the shadow of the flame, the exiled prince, anyone can betray anyone…</i> like 10 times in one single page and it made me want to punch someone. I kid you not, it was so repetitive and plain stupid. Aveyard tried so hard to make those names and quotes to work but they were way too much. It did not work.<br><br>I missed Evangeline. She was such a threat and she was fun to read. I actually missed ALL THE VILLAINS. While our, uhm, heroes were traveling and recruiting people, they were facing problems BUT none of Maven’s actions in this book were as bad as in book one. Same with the queen.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428717287ra/14474242.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Where did the evil masterminds go?</u> And because we didn’t have that <i>fast-pacing-we’re-going-to-die</i> kind of thing, we got plenty of time to read all about Mare’s breakdowns, yay.<br><br>On that note, the queen was killed so fucking easily I totally missed it. Like??? <b>Was that it?</b> It was not only ridiculous but such a disrespect to the image I had of the queen. I just can’t believe she was killed that easy, you know? I was waiting for her to get up and start making people kill each other on the plane but nope.<br><br>And I was bored. Utterly bored during the whole book. Like I said, I put it down several times because I honestly didn’t want to continue reading it. I felt like it was going nowhere and I hated that feeling. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442859289ra/16285415.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, what I actually LIKED? Cal.<br><br>I wanted Aveyard to explore him and let us know him better and she did. Thank you. He’s quite great and he really does not deserve Mare whatsoever. He’s so much more sensitive and strong than I thought he was and absolutely clever. He’s got a really sweet heart and he’s just so good. He could’ve been an amazing king.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441223583ra/16079840.gif" width="245" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If there was something done right in this book, that was Cal’s characterization. I fell for the guy big time and I truly hope he gets to be happy in the end.<br><br>The other thing I liked about this mess was Cameron, Shade and the very end. Yep, all that in one single category because the more I think about the book, the more pissed I get. <br><br>I think that Cameron was, not only a strong addition, but also someone who gave a new purpose to the plotline. She was on point with a lot of things that Mare, selfish stupid Mare, could not see.<br><br>Shade *sigh* I did not see it coming and I’m not happy about it. <br>Look, I’m more than okay with deaths, seriously BUT his dead only served to what…? So Mare could wake the fuck up and do some shit? That was… ugh, I have no words. I’m just pissed.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427849491ra/14327990.gif" width="500" height="235" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I appreciated what Shade added to the story and he was just a good guy. So no. I’m not happy with what happened to him but at the same time I’m happy I got to know him a bit more.<br><br><u>Was it me or Fayre whatever her name is acted weird? I mean, I’m not talking about Shade’s death but I got the feeling she was hiding something. Is she pregnant? Are all the newbloods dying or something? Not only I don’t know what was the answer to what the eye guy said to her but that fishy feeling is still there.</u><br><br>The end was unexpected? I mean, I knew Mare was going to pull a Tris Prior but I guess I didn’t expect Maven to treat her like a dog. I liked that. If Mare is stupid enough to suffer for that piece of shit, then she well deserves what’s coming to her.<br><br>I mean:<br><blockquote>
  <b> “I’m not blind. I watched you take the notes off the bodies. I thought you’d rip them up. But when you didn’t—I suppose I wanted to see what you were going to do. Burn them, throw them away, send them back dipped in Silver blood—but not keep them. Not read them while I slept next to you.”<br>“You said you missed him too. You said so,” I whisper. I have to refrain from stamping my foot like a frustrated child.<br>“He’s my brother. I miss him in a very different way.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Mare, I just…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451762662ra/17599947.gif" width="500" height="282" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aveyard’s storytelling did not improve either and I did not know if I was reading a sci-fi, paranormal or fantasy novel. I think it’s an issue when an author doesn’t have a particular style that fits with the genre they’re writing so that was a disappointment as well.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425506080ra/13899857.gif" width="320" height="178" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Will I read the last book? Yeah, probably. I’m curious to see how this mess of a story is going to continue but for now I just want to forget about this book.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15714052505842857502" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2306381079?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="jessica" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica">jessica</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2306381079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12886394153475586028">rounding up my rating because im in a good mood and still feeling that christmas cheer, but there are only so many rebel military tactics and kingdom overthrow attempts i can read before a book becomes a snooze fest. sigh. <br/><br/>this isnt as captivating as the <i>‘red queen’</i> (because of the aforementioned issues with boredom) but, because of that ending, i have my fingers crossed that the story can be redeemed in the next book. maybe this is just an unfortunate case of a sophomore slump, so im not giving</span>
  <span id="freeText12886394153475586028" style="display:none">rounding up my rating because im in a good mood and still feeling that christmas cheer, but there are only so many rebel military tactics and kingdom overthrow attempts i can read before a book becomes a snooze fest. sigh. <br /><br />this isnt as captivating as the <i>‘red queen’</i> (because of the aforementioned issues with boredom) but, because of that ending, i have my fingers crossed that the story can be redeemed in the next book. maybe this is just an unfortunate case of a sophomore slump, so im not giving up just yet!<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>3.5 stars</i></b></span>

YA GOTTA LOVE AN HONORABLE AND POWERFUL MAN IN UNIFORM.<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424490368i/13768503._SY540_.jpg' width='145' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Edit:</b><br/><br/><i>A little opinion of mine on why Maven will never be in the same category as the Darkling or Warner.</i><br/><br/> The Darkling is a villain who believes with all his heart that he is saving the Grisha and freeing the population from a tyrant (sadly he doesn't see that he's become a tyrant </span>
  <span id="freeText6303456321298705928" style="display:none">I AM WAITING FOR THIS BOOK. <br><br>Oh, and while Maven is interesting as a villain, he is no Darkling (my poor poor baby). With that said, I'm TEAM CAL ALL THE WAY BABY. YA GOTTA LOVE AN HONORABLE AND POWERFUL MAN IN UNIFORM.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424490368i/13768503._SY540_.jpg" width="145" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Edit:</b><br><br><i>A little opinion of mine on why Maven will never be in the same category as the Darkling or Warner.</i><br><br> The Darkling is a villain who believes with all his heart that he is saving the Grisha and freeing the population from a tyrant (sadly he doesn't see that he's become a tyrant himself in the process). While Maven is none of that. He has no charismatic appeal, is weak physically and mentally, and he cowardly hides behind his mother's skirts. Maven does the despicable things he does, knowing full well of their destruction, and he revels in it. <br><br> Warner might have killed, fully conscious of the immorality of the act, however, he takes no pleasure in killing. He does what has to be done, as he operates by his own code of justice, and [spoiler] to protect his mother. On the other hand, becoming a villain was Maven's grotesque version of being a petulant child: when he doesn't get what he wants, he lashes out at everyone. There is no noble goal, no disillusions about his actions. In fact, Cal, with his bloody acts and a stubborn mind on the righteousness of his philosophy, are much more Darkling-esque. So no, I wouldn't put Maven in the same category as those like Warner or the Darkling, because that would be grossly offensive to their amazing villain story.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11945196195096097121"><b> Full Review </b><br/><br/>Finally done with this mess. This is the most boring book I have read in my life and I rather watch paint try. An annoying main character did not help either. <br/><br/>Shoutout to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/62795872-alexander-hamilton' rel='nofollow noopener'>Maven's bish</a> for suffering with me. Almost DNF a lot of times but held on because of this buddy read.<br/><br/>I’ve never 1 stared a book.   <span id="freeText11945196195096097121" style="display:none"><b> Full Review </b><br /><br />Finally done with this mess. This is the most boring book I have read in my life and I rather watch paint try. An annoying main character did not help either. <br /><br />Shoutout to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/62795872-alexander-hamilton" rel="nofollow noopener">Maven's bish</a> for suffering with me. Almost DNF a lot of times but held on because of this buddy read.<br /><br />I’ve never 1 stared a book. I usually DNF books that I’m not enjoying but I kept reading this especially because people told me it gets better at the end but the end wasn’t enough for me to rate this book any higher. My buddy-read consisted of us complaining about how there was no point in this book and that the main character was annoying. <br /><br /><b> Things I hated </b><br />- Majority of this book is spent describing Mare and co going on field trips, trying to save people. It was so boring and I did not care about the journey at all. <br /><br />- Mare was so condescending and cocky: She treated her so-called best friend Kilorn like shit because he didn’t have any abilities. She talked to him like he was a child (even though he’s older than her) and was always trying to stop him from helping. I’m pretty sure she called him useless at some point. Imagine if it was a male character that said/treated a female character like that… Plus Mare thought she was God’s gift to earth. Her ability is good but there were people with better abilities than she and I don’t understand why she felt she was this special snowflake. <br /><br />- This book introduced too many characters, each of them having their own abilities. It was so hard figuring out who was who and I had to stop reading at some points to try and remember who the person that is being talked about is. It made it hard to care for any of the characters<br /><br />- Alot of irrelevant things are discussed at length but when it comes to something that is actually interesting, it doesn’t get discussed until after it happens… sometimes I thought that I was missing a page. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ there was no writing about how the queen got killed!! Like that was a main plot point but It just gets glanced over??????? And that scene when Maven captured them but they somehow escaped… I would have liked to read about those instead of being told after the fact  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />- Romance you say, What romance??? It doesn’t take me long to ship people, I have shipped two people before they even spoke to each other. In this, there was zero chemistry between the two love interest. I did not care about them at all and there was no other romance, except one little one which I didn’t really care about. So I’m still shipless and I’m bitter about it. I need my romance fix<br /><br />- I really don’t want to hear the phrase “anyone can betray anyone’ ever again<br /><br />- X-MEN did it better<br /><br /><b> Things I liked </b><br />- When someone was going off on Mare which unfortunately did not happen regularly.<br />- Cal<br /><br />How do you make a book about people with different awesome abilities so boring?? <br /><br />Maybe I hate myself because I still plan on finishing this series...</span>

<div id="review_1327823713" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1327823713" />
    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1327823713?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1327823713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10407304557274301629"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If I am a sword, I am a sword made of glass, beginning to shatter."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>This book ruined my life.<br/><br/>I HATED it.<br/><br/>But I LOVED it all the same.<br/><br/>I know that people either hate or love Red Queen but I really do believe that this series is slowing becoming its own. Red Queen was far from original and I still had lots of X-Men and Hunger Game vibes while reading Glass Sword but I still enjoyed this book nonetheless and I'm really looking forward to seeing this series evolve even more as the later bo</span>
  <span id="freeText10407304557274301629" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If I am a sword, I am a sword made of glass, beginning to shatter."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>This book ruined my life.<br /><br />I HATED it.<br /><br />But I LOVED it all the same.<br /><br />I know that people either hate or love Red Queen but I really do believe that this series is slowing becoming its own. Red Queen was far from original and I still had lots of X-Men and Hunger Game vibes while reading Glass Sword but I still enjoyed this book nonetheless and I'm really looking forward to seeing this series evolve even more as the later books come out.<br /><br />It took me awhile to get back into the story in the beginning because I couldn't remember certain details that happened in the last book so I strongly recommend rereading Red Queen before continuing onto Glass Sword. On top of that, it was a little slow at first but once the story picked up, I didn't have it in me to put the book down and I devoured it all in a matter hours.<br /><br />One thing I have to complain about was how often Victoria Aveyard was drilling "anyone can betray anyone" into our heads throughout the whole book. It got a bit annoying, really. I can understand mentioning it once or twice but we were constantly reminded in almost every chapter... Talk about overkill. We get it. Anyone can betray anyone. It took away the element of surprise for me because just like Mare, I doubted every single person. Maybe the author was trying to prove a point but if her goal was to pull some sort of reaction out of her readers like last time, it didn't really work out for me this time around because I was anticipating every little scenario possible.<br /><br />But other than that, I was fully immersed in the book.<br /><br />I was complaining that nothing was going on until it hit me in the face and now I'm suffering double time because I NEED MORE. This book wasn't enough.<br /><br />The characters in this book were awesome. Sometimes I wanted to slap some sense into some of them but I LOVED everyone and the new characters as well!<br /><br />SHADE. My heart. &lt;3<br /><br />And Farley being the badass that she is. Oh my aching heart.<br /><br />CAL. Moody, damaged, handsome prince. I loved him a thousand times more in this book.<br /><br />MAVEN. THERE WASN'T ENOUGH MAVEN. WHY!!!!<br /><br />And oh um... Queen Elara. Was I the only one thinking WHEN???? I was literally like... "Wait. What." *Flips back pages* WHAT. I might've missed when it happened or maybe I just got too excited but I just have one word to say about it: ANTICLIMACTIC.<br /><br />Now I have to wait another year. Sigh. I'm still torn on who I love more: Maven or Cal. I feel like it's The Grisha trilogy all over again except I actually love both male characters. I want Mare to end up with Maven but at the same time I want Maven to myself so Mare can end up with Cal. But I want the moody, misplaced prince too... I guess I'm fine with whoever she ends up with because I love them both!<br /><br />But anyways, I need the next book and I need it now. Please and thank you. So much happened. Maybe even too much, but at the same time not enough. This series just keeps getting better and I'm already so hyped up for the next one!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10407304557274301629" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1554437077" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1554437077" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1554437077?book_show_action=true">Feb 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780062455321" href="/book/show/26531536-glass-sword">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=owned-physical-copy">owned-physical-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=strong-female-characters">strong-female-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=young-adult-fantasy">young-adult-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=fangirling">fangirling</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1554437077" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12574177594849447139">Gripping, intense, and an achingly beautiful comeback. This sequel to the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22328546.Red_Queen__Red_Queen___1_' title='Red Queen (Red Queen, #1) by Victoria Aveyard' rel='nofollow noopener'>Red Queen</a> is <b>Victoria Aveyard at her very best!</b><br/><br/>Sequels have always been very crucial in a series because they can either be a success, a failure, or in between. Thankfully, this sequel fell to the success side.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456644632ra/18260372.gif' width='350' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/> <b>Red Queen</b> ended up with a promise. <b>Glass Sword</b> started off by fulfilling that promise.<br/><br/>It's actually hard not to love this book because first and foremost, everything started with a BANG! Lots of actions were already</span>
  <span id="freeText12574177594849447139" style="display:none">Gripping, intense, and an achingly beautiful comeback. This sequel to the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22328546.Red_Queen__Red_Queen___1_" title="Red Queen (Red Queen, #1) by Victoria Aveyard" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Queen</a> is <b>Victoria Aveyard at her very best!</b><br><br>Sequels have always been very crucial in a series because they can either be a success, a failure, or in between. Thankfully, this sequel fell to the success side.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456644632ra/18260372.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Red Queen</b> ended up with a promise. <b>Glass Sword</b> started off by fulfilling that promise.<br><br>It's actually hard not to love this book because first and foremost, everything started with a BANG! Lots of actions were already happening even at the very first pages that I found myself gripping the edge of my seat.<br><br>I was particularly amazed by how Victoria Aveyard weaved the plotline of this book with so much <b>thrill and adventure</b>. The searching for <i>new bloods</i> and the painful, action-packed experiences Mare and the gang experienced as they journeyed from places to places. The <b>introduction of new characters</b> that are so interesting and with unique traits and abilities. So exceptional!<br><br>Yes, <b>there were parts that are dragging</b>, but who cares? They actually gave so much time to take it all in and anticipate what's about to come. Was I surprised? Hell, yes! There were so many shocking scenes and revelations here. Even heartbreaking ones that made me cry.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I stare at the polished metal, examining my reflection. The girl I see is both familiar and foreign, Mare, Mareena, the lightning girl, the Red queen, and no one at all. She does not look afraid. She looks carved of stone, with severer features, hair braided tight to her head, and a tangle of scars on her neck. She is not seventeen, but ageless, Silver but not, Red but not, human--but not. A banner of the Scarlet Guard, a face on a wanted poster, a prince's downfall, a thief... a killer. A doll who can take any form but her own."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Mare's character development, I admit, was kind of an on-and-off here. Sometimes she was so weak and hopeless but most of the time her strength was the one that made sense to everything. On the other hand, <b>Cal</b>-- <i>Holy freakin' Cal!</i> This guy-- *sigh This brooding prince, ONCE AGAIN, swept me off my feet! <b>His character development</b> in this book amazed me to no end! Seriously, I love him even better here! He was indeed born a leader as the way he acted always had an air of command. And when he brought the <i>"That's my girl"</i> line to Mare.... *squeals! Who wouldn't swoon over?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456646330ra/18260503.gif" width="300" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The <b>romantic</b> parts in this book was my most favorite, of course. I was so happy that there was a bit of a romantic development here between Mare and Cal! MY SHIP! It was certainly sailing in all its glory!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456646747ra/18260529.gif" width="350" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending, however, made me flinch and cry and feel a bit of frustrated. WHAT ON EARTH JUST HAPPENED? I was screaming at the top of my lungs because once again, CLIFFHANGER! And we all have to wait another year before the third book comes out!<br><br>All in all, Glass Sword is a beautiful, satisfying, made-me-swoon-and-cry sequel. Everything that happened here was remarkable and right in target.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"If I am a sword, I am a sword made of glass, and I feel myself beginning to shatter."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Rating: <br><br>5 Stars<br><br><p>
  <a href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446199662i/16763926._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pearl's Book Journey (1)" width="380" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993261i/16730770.jpg" width="200" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1564721449" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1564721449" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44125660-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600268807p2/44125660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1564721449?book_show_action=true">Feb 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/44125660-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=nope">nope</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=series-not-continuing">series-not-continuing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=1-star">1-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1564721449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1864989433119447589"><b>DNF at 64%, page 286</b><br/><br/><i>Just to pre-warn everyone, I'm in a bit of a ranty mode.</i><br/><br/>I've finally had to call it quits. I just feel so let down by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23174274.Glass_Sword__Red_Queen___2_' title='Glass Sword (Red Queen, #2) by Victoria Aveyard' rel='nofollow noopener'>Glass Sword</a> after <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22328546.Red_Queen__Red_Queen___1_' title='Red Queen (Red Queen, #1) by Victoria Aveyard' rel='nofollow noopener'>Red Queen</a> was so good. Understandably after the way things turned out in the first book, it had to change direction. But how much it did, I just wasn't impressed. This book had so much potential. It's taken me FIVE days to read nearly 300 pages. That isn't like me at all.<br/><br/>My issues with this book are solely around Mare... I just didn't like he</span>
  <span id="freeText1864989433119447589" style="display:none"><b>DNF at 64%, page 286</b><br /><br /><i>Just to pre-warn everyone, I'm in a bit of a ranty mode.</i><br /><br />I've finally had to call it quits. I just feel so let down by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23174274.Glass_Sword__Red_Queen___2_" title="Glass Sword (Red Queen, #2) by Victoria Aveyard" rel="nofollow noopener">Glass Sword</a> after <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22328546.Red_Queen__Red_Queen___1_" title="Red Queen (Red Queen, #1) by Victoria Aveyard" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Queen</a> was so good. Understandably after the way things turned out in the first book, it had to change direction. But how much it did, I just wasn't impressed. This book had so much potential. It's taken me FIVE days to read nearly 300 pages. That isn't like me at all.<br /><br />My issues with this book are solely around Mare... I just didn't like her what so ever in this book, she is so self centred and seems to put herself before anyone else. I hated, literally <b>hated</b> how she treated Cal and Kilorn. Particularly that she underestimated Kilorn for not being "special". I mean <i>come on</i> up until a few months prior they were both from the Stilts as Reds with no known ability. It was just so infuriating. Not just that, but she always seemed to want to be right, like she doesn't listen to advice or offer support to anyone who she <u>knows</u> needs it. <b>Infuriating</b><br /><br />As for the plot? It started off so strong, I can hold my hands up and say I was blown away by the first few chapters, I thought it was smart and it had <u>so much potential</u>. After that, for me personally it kind of dwindled. Personally I usually like some deceit it books, I mean who doesn't like a twist? But the fact is, I feel like it pushes you not to trust anyone in this book. Why would you not want to like anyone?! It seems that the book is full to the brim and the characters are constantly doing something, but my question is. What?! It just seems to me that it's a lot of walking around and searching with not much else.<br /><br />It also doesn't have a lot of character development. All we seem to get is Mare. You know what? I couldn't stand her. I know I've said this. But I honestly couldn't. All we see is her. I don't know how the book continues, but I would of loved to see more of Shade. He was one character that really stood out for me, and he was barely in it!<br /><br />Cal is literally thrown to the side and treated horrifically, even though time and time again he proves his worth. It's just so infuriating. <i>His bright flame has grown dark indeed"</i> well of course it has you fool, look at how he's being treated!<br /><br /><b>What <u>did</u> I like?</b><br />- Shade and Cal were honestly the only redeeming features for me. <br />- Maybe the first few chapters as well...<br /><br />Overall, it just got to the point where I was forcing myself to read it, simply for the fact I wanted to continue the series and find out what happens in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30226723.King_s_Cage__Red_Queen___3_" title="King's Cage (Red Queen, #3) by Victoria Aveyard" rel="nofollow noopener">King's Cage</a>. I told myself at the start of the year, if I don't enjoy a book, don't finish it. So I'm sticking to that. Maybe in the future I will try again, but for now? <b>No thank you.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1864989433119447589" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1886391466" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1886391466" />
    <a title="~Poppy~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/59201076-poppy"><img alt="~Poppy~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572358822p2/59201076.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1886391466?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Poppy~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Poppy~" href="/user/show/59201076-poppy">~Poppy~</a>
      </span>

        rated it

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1561114750?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9780062417305" href="/book/show/25741639-glass-sword">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=revenge-stories">revenge-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1561114750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9039510442345115081">The second book in the series, 'Glass Sword' picks up where 'Red Queen' left off. Mare and Cal are on the run with The Scarlet Guard, as they regroup and plan their next move. It doesn't take long for this story to get more complicated once they begin their missions to save the other "new bloods" and bring down the king.<br/><br/>Although this time around Mare and Cal seemed to grow closer, there still wasn't enough romance for me. I enjoyed the action and adventure, but I craved a deeper, more emotional </span>
  <span id="freeText9039510442345115081" style="display:none">The second book in the series, 'Glass Sword' picks up where 'Red Queen' left off. Mare and Cal are on the run with The Scarlet Guard, as they regroup and plan their next move. It doesn't take long for this story to get more complicated once they begin their missions to save the other "new bloods" and bring down the king.<br /><br />Although this time around Mare and Cal seemed to grow closer, there still wasn't enough romance for me. I enjoyed the action and adventure, but I craved a deeper, more emotional connection between these two. At times, they seemed to be getting closer. Then, they'd turn their backs on each other with little thought or consideration. That drove me crazy!<br /><br />I listened to the Audible version of this story and it continues to be well-narrated. There is a lot going on in this story, so I did find myself needing to rewind a few times to catch details that I missed. However, that was a result of my own distraction and not a failure of the narrators to engage me in the story.<br /><br />Overall, I think that this story continues to be good. It wasn't as good as the first book, for me, but I still liked it. I will continue the series when the next book is released. I give it 3 1/2 stars. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9039510442345115081" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1113268493" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1113268493" />
    <a title="Katerina  Kondrenko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36306002-katerina-kondrenko"><img alt="Katerina  Kondrenko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590049412p2/36306002.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1113268493?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina  Kondrenko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina  Kondrenko" href="/user/show/36306002-katerina-kondrenko">Katerina  Kondrenko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">even those who disliked Red Queen</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=10-out-of-10">10-out-of-10</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=pov-female-only">pov-female-only</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=genre-fantasy">genre-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=ships-mine-is-sailing">ships-mine-is-sailing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=writing-suspesful-as-hell">writing-suspesful-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=pov-1st-person">pov-1st-person</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=mood-cry-me-a-river">mood-cry-me-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=ships-have-two-or-more">ships-have-two-or-more</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=characters-relatable-ones">characters-relatable-ones</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=characters-prince-fetish-shelf">characters-prince-fetish-shelf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1113268493" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8002892924263056102"><b>
  <blockquote>9.5 out of 10</blockquote>
</b><br/><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br/><a href='http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/12/glass-sword-by-victoria-aveyard.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br/><br/><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qLXMH-EJGVQ' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Spiritual Machines – Couldn't Stop Caring</a><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=u83vXU0um_A' rel='nofollow noopener'>That Winter, The Wind Blows – Blind Love</a><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LePBbaYfqeo' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tyrone Wells – Remain</a><br/><br/><b>Genre: </b>fantasy, dystopia, YA<br/><b>Stuff: </b>civil war, war, superpowers, usurper, Silvers vs. Reds<br/><b>WOW: </b>writing-style, relationships between characters<br/><b>POV: </b>1st-person, fema</span>
  <span id="freeText8002892924263056102" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>9.5 out of 10</blockquote>
</b><br><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br><a href="http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/12/glass-sword-by-victoria-aveyard.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br><br><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qLXMH-EJGVQ" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Spiritual Machines – Couldn't Stop Caring</a><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=u83vXU0um_A" rel="nofollow noopener">That Winter, The Wind Blows – Blind Love</a><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LePBbaYfqeo" rel="nofollow noopener">Tyrone Wells – Remain</a><br><br><b>Genre: </b>fantasy, dystopia, YA<br><b>Stuff: </b>civil war, war, superpowers, usurper, Silvers vs. Reds<br><b>WOW: </b>writing-style, relationships between characters<br><b>POV: </b>1st-person, female<br><b>Love-Geometry: </b>seeming<br><br><b>Quote-Core: </b><i>
  "We seem weak because we want to."
</i><br> <br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-bDcN-0PUQq4/Vnkxbkz1GtI/AAAAAAAAAUg/TdD15qUdT_E/s1600/collage_photocat.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="120" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450786172i/17469482._SX540_.jpg" width="640" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Can I just say that this book is the most unexpected thing I've read in this year?</b> I liked <i>Red Queen</i>, I did, but there were flaws and holes, and between 'like' and 'love' is an abyss. Now listen, I loved <i>Glass Sword</i>. I didn't plan to, my heart was closed, but Victoria rose red as the dawn, and I fell in awe with an ache in my chest. If she would improve herself further, I don't know what we'll get with the last book in this series. A heart-attack, maybe?<br><br>This installment picks up right there the previous one ended: we are underground and we try to escape Maven's evil grip. The first chapter (which you could already read) is a chaos, mist and what's-going-ons, but hold on tight, this is only the beginning. <i>Glass Sword</i> would let us see more of Scarlet Guard, we'll fly, we'll meet newbloods with bad-ass powers, we'll fight, we'll win, we'll lose and so on. This book is an action and emotion-packed one. Yes, you've heard me right. Emotions. I hadn't any intention to shift at my seat or passing across the room, or screaming at characters, swoon over them, be afraid or happy, or sad. But Victoria wrote her book with so intense words... <b>There's a soul between the pages</b>.<br><br>It's a shame I can't show you any quotes, rules are rules and I have to wait until February. Though maybe that's better this way, 'cause every page is a twist. Twist upon twist. Don't forget about anyone can betray anyone. Beware.<br><br>We know that second books in series are often a bit of meh. I thought it would be the same with <i>Glass Sword</i>. Boring recruiting, games with Maven, ruined love-ship with Cal, Kilorn's presence, Guards... I considered these things boring. Boy was I wrong. Yes, this book is its genre's child and you can predict the plot's frame, but what lies in between is always an ocean of choices and possibilities. You would be soothed with delusory familiar passing, but this is what Victoria needs to clap her hands near your ear and make you jump when you least expect it. Anything can happen with anyone (yes, now I love to use such constructions, haha).<br><br><b>Romantic line</b> would be so subtle! But if you look closer, you'd get burned from the heat that is there. Everyone, who knows me well, is aware of which prince is my fav. It's Cal and there will be enough of this fire man in <i>Glass Sword</i>. His ship with Mare isn't that broken, but it's not a whole boat either. These two made me suffer and happy and crazy and so much more at the same time. The thing they shared is a beauty itself. They are my OTP and that's it.<br><br><b>Mare </b>have changed. Now she is strong, reasonable, ruthless and willing to do something, to help her nation, to avenge herself. Not at the start, but she would get how tangled life is, how hard to tell allies from enemies, how impossible to please everyone or to save every single person, how high the price of revolutions is. I'm not sure whether I like her or not. Yet. But I admire her sometimes. I see why she does what she does. The only thing I would never forgive her is Cal. One wrong word, one wrong move and I'm ready to smack this girl with a chair. All of us has some flaws, Mare's biggest one are double-standards. What is allowed to others isn't allowed to Cal. Until the end I was waiting for the tiniest sign, which could show me her true feelings for him, if there were some to begin with. I speak not about kisses or even words... I needed an act, a metaphor. Did I get one? Oh, you'll see.<br><br><b>Cal</b>... my beloved exiled prince. He was left with nothing. They took his past (mother, the way he saw things), his present (father, home, power), his future (throne, which would never be his even with Maven being defeated), but he didn't become weak or a rude bastard. Hated among Silvers, hated among Reds. They accused him in all the bad things Silvers made to Reads, they punched him with fists and words, but he stayed still, he didn't hurt them back, he didn't leave. Why? Oh, don't tell me you have no idea why. And after such acts of his... I fell for him so hard that I broke some bones of mine. He's a MAN. Even Mare was bitching him sometimes, but he never did the same in reward. People didn't get how he felt himself, what he had lost, that every war has both than one truth, both sides have their own versions of event, their own reasons. And he didn't press his vision on them, he was helping those people, he was grateful and nice. I can't tell you more without spoilers, I just wanna make you feel how I love this boy. If Maven is a man of his word, then Cal is man of his act.<br><br>Well, <b>Maven</b>... our Darkling-ish little bitch. Forget the boy you may love in <i>Red Queen</i> and meet a new one: cold, calculating, merciless, cruel, obsessive. Yes, obsessive with Mare. He wanted her dead not a long time ago, but now he wants simply... her. And the throne, of course. Maven won't be an often guest on <i>Glass Sword's</i> pages but he would be always there. Nor Mare, neither Cal would be able to forget the boy they loved (or, in Mare's case, was ready to love) so soon. They would ache for Maven who wasn't exist to begin with. Thus he would remain in their thoughts, between their bodies, inside their hearts. While his physical self would try to hunt them down. Goosebumps... <br><br><b>Other characters</b> were great as well. I loved Mare's brothers, especially Shade. Loved even Farley, though I wasn't her fan before. It was good to see more people with different abilities, to see more of the world-building, to learn more secrets. Now I know how wide Victoria's plan is, how far her imagination is going to march. I would be there to touch it, to taste it and to enjoy.<br><br>Again, I wanna praise the <b>writing-style</b>. At some moments I was weeping so hard... my mother, who set next to me, was shocked. Maybe it's me and my sensitive nature, but I think it's Victoria words and how she tells her story. I swear people, you have to be ready.<br><br>The <b>final</b> had blown my mind. I didn't know I would give the book around 10 stars until the very last page. It was 8 then 9, then 8 or 9, and then BOOM 9.5 STARS. My heart was pounding, my mouth was open and my eyes were swollen from tears while I was suddenly sure what to do, how to rate and didn't know how to survive 'til the next book. Victoria, what have you done? *cries again*<br><br><b>Red Queen (Алая королева):</b><br><blockquote>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1219807950" rel="nofollow noopener">Queen Song (Песнь королевы)</a> #0.1/4<br>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1312174580" rel="nofollow noopener">Steel Scars (Стальные шрамы)</a> #0.2/4<br>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1113268481" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Queen</a> (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1469225994" rel="nofollow noopener">Алая Королева</a>) #1/4<br>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1113268493" rel="nofollow noopener">Glass Sword (Стеклянный меч</a>) #2/4<br>— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1113268496" rel="nofollow noopener">King's Cage (Королевская клетка)</a> #3/4<br>— Untitled (Без названия) #4/4</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="8002892924263056102" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2004002379" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2004002379" />
    <a title="Always Pouting" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48650982-always-pouting"><img alt="Always Pouting" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483476563p2/48650982.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2004002379?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Always Pouting" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Always Pouting" href="/user/show/48650982-always-pouting">Always Pouting</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25645546-glass-sword">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2004002379" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8451091131755281804">After Mare and Cal manage to escape execution, Maven begins to relentlessly hunt them. Which wouldn't be so bad if they were going to stay on the secured island they're hiding out at, courtesy of the Scarlet Guard, but alas there is the problem of the New Bloods. Mare and Cal must race against Maven to get to the New Bloods before he can kill them, as well as figure out a place to keep and train them. The two also must try to deal with the fall out from Maven's betrayal and their feelings for on</span>
  <span id="freeText8451091131755281804" style="display:none">After Mare and Cal manage to escape execution, Maven begins to relentlessly hunt them. Which wouldn't be so bad if they were going to stay on the secured island they're hiding out at, courtesy of the Scarlet Guard, but alas there is the problem of the New Bloods. Mare and Cal must race against Maven to get to the New Bloods before he can kill them, as well as figure out a place to keep and train them. The two also must try to deal with the fall out from Maven's betrayal and their feelings for one another that played a part in causing their exile from the kingdom. <br /><br />I actually enjoyed this more than I did Red Queen, it was fun to read about the other powers that Reds could have. I still want a better idea for where this is coming from or what is happening but there was some progress on that front as well here so I'm satisfied for now. Farley and Kilorn were great, not that I didn't like them in the first one but this one only let me enjoy them much more and now I'm like completely attached to them. I wouldn't mind getting to have more plot line with the New Bloods though because as of right now I don't really care as much about them but that's a later problem. <br /><br />I see that people still hate Mare, the love of my life, but I still love her. Yeah she spent the whole first book whining but as a fellow whiner I think it was the appropriate course of action, especially considering how shit life was for her. Also I get that maybe her hero complex seems self centered but it feels slightly justified because she is the only New Blood people are familiar with already and the most powerful person as of this moment. Anyway Mare is still the best and as kayne once said I don't care what none of y'all say I still love her.<br /><br />I still think Cal is amazingly boring though and I couldn't care less about his romance with Mare. I feel like I should be swooning or something but I'm kind of just like why is Cal still around. Not that Maven is much better, please someone tell me he dies soon because I'm sick of him. I'm just going to go read the third one right now because I need to know what happened. Fingers crossed that Maven dies a fiery painful death.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8451091131755281804" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
