<div id="review_1070442616" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1070442616" />
    <a title="Giselle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5789353-giselle"><img alt="Giselle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605042512p2/5789353.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1070442616?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Giselle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Giselle" href="/user/show/5789353-giselle">Giselle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=age-young-adult">age-young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=borrowed">borrowed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-fantasy">genre-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-dystopia">genre-dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=2-star">2-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-science-fiction">genre-science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-romance">genre-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1070442616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6212350333749248456">All things considered, this is a book I should like. A book I would gobble up in one sitting and ask for the next one in a hurry, but I can't. I am so annoyed. The pacing for me was too weak at points because I found myself skimming over some paragraphs just trying to read it faster than normal.<br/><br/>I was irritated with Mare the main character the whole time. It could be due to the fact that she keeps repeating how much of a weapon she is, and how she will destroy the world if she releases all her po</span>
  <span id="freeText6212350333749248456" style="display:none">All things considered, this is a book I should like. A book I would gobble up in one sitting and ask for the next one in a hurry, but I can't. I am so annoyed. The pacing for me was too weak at points because I found myself skimming over some paragraphs just trying to read it faster than normal.<br /><br />I was irritated with Mare the main character the whole time. It could be due to the fact that she keeps repeating how much of a weapon she is, and how she will destroy the world if she releases all her power. Another reason is that she denies even saying goodbye to her own family, and trusts the "enemy" more so than her own best friend whom she's known most of her life. And then there's the fact that she is spiralling down this dark and sinister path. Did she not have any questions about why the heck she's both a Red and Silver? Why isn't she questioning this? And if she is, then how about her brother? And why is she not doing everything in her power to save every Red blood from the clutches of the Silver government. She only starts to act once Cameron tells her so. Is this the path that she's supposed to take? To become like them? If it is, I'm hoping she gets her priorities straight. Her family should mean the world to her. And her friends. But she is too much of a romantic for me. Swooning over these two boys, it was a little too much for me. I was not a fan.<br /><br />Then there was the whole recruitment process and all, and at first it was a little boring, I wanted to stop reading but then I kept going once someone told me the ending ends on a cliffhanger. I love cliffhanger endings so I decided to plow on. It was fun reading about everyone's new powers no one has seen before. That was my favourite part. Then the ending FINALLY came and I was a little disappointed because I wanted a twist or surprise but there wasn't one. It's too simple to predict that ending because clues are given throughout the whole story. <br /><br />So yes this was problematic for me to read, but on the other hand it wasn't due to the writing or the world, it was the characters themselves. It's always hard to like a book when some characters irritate you. <br /><br />I'm still pretty interested in how this whole series ends only because I want to know what happens. Who will win the war? And will peace finally reign all over the countries? That's what I'm eager to find out.<br /><br />RATING 2/5<br /><br />QUOTES<br /><br />Strange, my enemies know me best, and my family doesn't know me at all. (67)<br /><br />I curl inward and bleed alone, inside where no one else can see. (70)<br /><br />We seem weak because we want to. (79)<br /><br />Anyone can betray anyone. (87)<br /><br />There's nothing wrong with us. We're different, yes, but not wrong. And certainly not better. (99)<br /><br />What's your ability, dear? Superhuman rudeness? (219)</span>
  <a data-text-id="6212350333749248456" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TvahihJf/H3NiRtn09ZPiuj//pL6jKxQOgr2CfuVnSloScYY6V4Rz2Ekia38Zt5W7cxmCvCXEKwp/UVE2yeBvw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zKBMjy0Xcz/6SJ2O5sAbTWyJCKj0QvwZ9wc3ZXQpeqzqHysd1haejVblD0TJcIqRabqQMP5ZQOXk8IQoVJtmOg==')})
  }
